# Process Improvement Tracking

This file tracks the status of process improvements identified through feedback collection and tools review in the project.

## Status Legend

| Status               | Description                                                         | Next Task      |
| -------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------- | -------------- |
| Needs Prioritization | Improvement opportunity identified, needs evaluation and prioritization | PF-TSK-009 |
| Needs Implementation | Improvement evaluated and prioritized, ready for implementation     | Per IMP notes  |
| In Progress          | Improvement is currently being implemented                          | —              |
| Completed            | Improvement has been implemented and validated                      | —              |
| Deferred             | Improvement has been postponed to a later time                      | —              |
| Delegated            | Improvement requires a different task scope (e.g., PF-TSK-001, PF-TSK-014, PF-TSK-048) | Per IMP notes |
| Rejected             | Improvement was evaluated but determined not to be beneficial       | —              |

## Task Routing

When [Process Improvement (PF-TSK-009)](/process-framework/tasks/support/process-improvement-task.md) evaluates an IMP, it routes to the appropriate task based on the solution type:

| Solution Type | Task | When |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Content update to existing file | [Process Improvement (PF-TSK-009)](/process-framework/tasks/support/process-improvement-task.md) | Adding callouts, fixing templates, updating guidance, process refinement |
| Structural change | [Structure Change (PF-TSK-014)](/process-framework/tasks/support/structure-change-task.md) | Moving/renaming files or directories, reorganizing sections, template changes affecting multiple files, metadata structure changes, information architecture evolution |
| New framework capability | [Framework Extension (PF-TSK-048)](/process-framework/tasks/support/framework-extension-task.md) | Multi-component extensions requiring new tasks + templates + scripts + guides, new workflows, new domains of functionality |

## Active Pilots

Pilots are Framework Extensions whose new behavior is being validated in a small set of representative artifacts before broader rollout. Pilot rows consume IDs from the same `PF-IMP-NNN` pool as Current Improvement Opportunities — a pilot is "an IMP with a multi-stage lifecycle". Concept docs for in-flight pilots remain in `process-framework-local/proposals/` (the temp state file archives at Phase 5 normally). When a pilot reaches `Resolved`, [Update-ProcessImprovement.ps1](/process-framework/scripts/update/Update-ProcessImprovement.ps1) archives the concept doc to `proposals/old/` and moves the pilot row from this section to **Completed Improvements** (mirrors regular IMP completion flow — PF-IMP-729). See [PF-PRO-030 — Framework Extension Pilot Tracking](../../proposals/old/framework-extension-pilot-tracking.md) for the lifecycle design.

**Status:**
- `Active` — Pilot in flight; adopters running and/or decision trigger awaiting resolution.
- `Resolved` — Rollout/rollback decision recorded; concept doc archived.

| ID | Source | Started | Adopters | Success Criteria | Decision Trigger | Status | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

## Priority Criteria

Improvements are prioritized based on:

1. **Frequency** - How often the issue appears in feedback
2. **Impact** - Potential improvement to efficiency or quality
3. **Effort** - Resources required for implementation
4. **Risk** - Potential negative consequences if not addressed

## Tasks That Update This File

The following tasks update this state file:

- [Tools Review Task](../../../process-framework/tasks/support/tools-review-task.md): Updates when improvements are identified, prioritized, or completed
- [Process Improvement Task](../../../process-framework/tasks/support/process-improvement-task.md): Updates when implementing larger process changes
- [Structure Change Task](../../../process-framework/tasks/support/structure-change-task.md): Updates when implementing structure changes
- [Framework Extension Task](../../../process-framework/tasks/support/framework-extension-task.md): Updates when adding new framework capabilities

The literal pattern .git/objects/<2-hex>/<38-hex> should never appear in tracked project files (only in .git internals). | 2026-04-30 | Rejected PF-IMP-683: Rejected after Step 5 evaluation. Concern: a same-Location + token-similarity warning would fire on legitimate similar TDs in the same file (multiple bare-except findings, multiple parser-quality items, etc.), creating warning noise that agents would learn to ignore — and once ignored, the rare real duplicate slips through anyway. One historical incident (TE-TAR-066, 5 duplicates) is insufficient to justify that ongoing cost. The cleanup of the actual incident took ~35 min; the proposed mechanism would impose recurring cognitive load on every -Add invocation indefinitely. Rejection rationale validated against real data: token-Jaccard >=0.4 catches all 5 known duplicates but inherently cannot distinguish them from legitimate same-file similar work without semantic understanding the script does not have. | AI Agent (PF-TSK-009) |

| 2026-05-04 | Rejected PF-IMP-715: Rejected after Step 6 evaluation. Cited Anthropic quote (CRITICAL: You MUST use this tool when... -> Use this tool when...) is real but applies specifically to tool/skill triggering on Opus 4.5/4.6, not framework process discipline.
